PER_Iranian_elections_decision_category = {
	PER_auto_update_gui_weekly = {
		allowed = { always = no }
		available = { always = no }
		fire_only_once = no
		is_good = yes
		selectable_mission = no
		days_mission_timeout = 7

		timeout_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { original_tag = PER }
				hidden_effect = {
					PER_scripted_effect_update_principalists_popularity_variable = yes
					if = { #8th Period
						limit = {
								date > 2001.6.1
								date < 2002.7.1
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = {
									var = principalists_popularity_percent
									value = 50
									compare = greater_than_or_equals
								}
							}
							country_event = {
								id = PER_election_events.9
								days = 0
							}
						}
						else = {
							country_event = {
								id = PER_election_events.8
								days = 0
							}
						}

					}
					else_if = { #9th Period
						limit = {
								date > 2005.6.9
								date < 2006.7.1
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = {
									var = principalists_popularity_percent
									value = 50
									compare = greater_than_or_equals
								}
							}
							country_event = {
								id = PER_election_events.11
								days = 0
							}
						}
						else = {
							country_event = {
								id = PER_election_events.10
								days = 0
							}
						}
					}
					else_if = { #10th Period
						limit = {
								date > 2009.6.5
								date < 2010.7.1
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = {
									var = principalists_popularity_percent
									value = 50
									compare = greater_than_or_equals
								}
							}
							country_event = {
								id = PER_election_events.13
								days = 0
							}
						}
						else = {
							country_event = {
								id = PER_election_events.12
								days = 0
							}
						}
					}
					else_if = { #11th Period
						limit = {
								date > 2013.6.7
								date < 2014.7.1
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = {
									var = principalists_popularity_percent
									value = 50
									compare = greater_than_or_equals
								}
							}
							if = {
								limit = {
									has_country_flag = principalist_portrait_ghalibaf
								}
								country_event = {
									id = PER_election_events.15
									days = 0
								}
							}
							else = {
								country_event = {
									id = PER_election_events.16
									days = 0
								}
							}
						}
						else = {
							country_event = {
								id = PER_election_events.14
								days = 0
							}
						}
					}
					else_if = { #12th Period
						limit = {
								date > 2017.5.12
								date < 2018.6.1
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = {
									var = principalists_popularity_percent
									value = 50
									compare = greater_than_or_equals
								}
							}
							country_event = {
								id = PER_election_events.18
								days = 0
							}
						}
						else = {
							country_event = {
								id = PER_election_events.17
								days = 0
							}
						}
					}
					else_if = { #13th Period
						limit = {
								date > 2021.6.11
								date < 2022.7.1
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = {
									var = principalists_popularity_percent
									value = 50
									compare = greater_than_or_equals
								}
							}
							country_event = {
								id = PER_election_events.20
								days = 0
							}
						}
						else = {
							country_event = {
								id = PER_election_events.19
								days = 0
							}
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_country_flag = PER_election_enabled
						}
						activate_mission = PER_auto_update_gui_weekly
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

PER_soleimani = {
	PER_mount_international_pressure = {

		icon = decision_generic_civil_support

		visible = {
			original_tag = PER
		}

		cost = 20
		days_remove = 3
		fire_only_once = yes

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision PER_mount_international_pressure"
			add_political_power = 40
		}

		remove_effect = {
			set_country_flag = mount_international_pressure
			USA = {
				add_political_power = -50
				add_stability = -0.05
			}
		}
	}
	PER_complain_to_the_united_nations = {

		icon = decision_generic_decision

			original_tag = PER

		cost = 50
		days_remove = 15
		fire_only_once = yes

			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision PER_complain_to_the_united_nationss"
			add_war_support = 0.02
		}

		remove_effect = {
			set_country_flag = complain_to_the_united_nations

				add_political_power = -75
			}
		}
	}

		fire_only_once = yes

		complete_effect = {

					israel_has_more_than_1_influence_trigger = yes

	PER_launch_missile = {
		allowed = {
			tag = PER
		}

		available = {
			original_tag = PER
			has_country_flag = mission_country_selected
			NOT = {
				has_decision = PER_launch_drone_attack
				has_decision = PER_capture_israeli_officials
				has_decision = PER_assassinate_israeli_agents
				has_decision = PER_ask_hashd_al_shaabi_to_raid_israeli_bases
				has_decision = PER_ask_houthis_to_raid_israeli_bases
				has_decision = PER_ask_huseyniyyun_to_raid_israeli_bases
			}
			hidden_trigger = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { PER_mission_country = IRQ.id }
					}
					OR = {
						var:PER_mission_country = {
							israel_has_more_than_1_influence_trigger = yes
						}
						KUR = {
							israel_has_more_than_1_influence_trigger = yes
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					var:PER_mission_country = {
						israel_has_more_than_1_influence_trigger = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}

		visible = {

		}

				check_variable = { missile_inventory_array^12 > 4 }
				check_variable = { missile_inventory_array^13 > 4 }
				check_variable = { missile_inventory_array^14 > 4 }
				check_variable = { missile_inventory_array^15 > 4 }

				check_variable = { missile_inventory_array^18 > 4 }
			}
		}

		days_re_enable = 100
		fire_only_once = no

		complete_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = remove_5_icbm_tt
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { missile_inventory_array^11 > 4 } } subtract_from_variable = { var = missile_inventory_array^11 value = 5 } } #Removes 5 ICBM missiles
			else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { missile_inventory_array^12 > 4 } } subtract_from_variable = { var = missile_inventory_array^12 value = 5 } } #Removes 5 ICBM missiles
			else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { missile_inventory_array^13 > 4 } } subtract_from_variable = { var = missile_inventory_array^13 value = 5 } } #Removes 5 ICBM missiles
			else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { missile_inventory_array^14 > 4 } } subtract_from_variable = { var = missile_inventory_array^14 value = 5 } } #Removes 5 ICBM missiles
			else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { missile_inventory_array^15 > 4 } } subtract_from_variable = { var = missile_inventory_array^15 value = 5 } } #Removes 5 ICBM missiles
			else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { missile_inventory_array^16 > 4 } } subtract_from_variable = { var = missile_inventory_array^16 value = 5 } } #Removes 5 ICBM missiles
			else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { missile_inventory_array^17 > 4 } } subtract_from_variable = { var = missile_inventory_array^17 value = 5 } } #Removes 5 ICBM missiles
			else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { missile_inventory_array^18 > 4 } } subtract_from_variable = { var = missile_inventory_array^18 value = 5 } } #Removes 5 ICBM missiles
		}
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision PER_launch_missile"

PER_brain_drain_removal = {
	PER_brain_drain_removal_4 = {

		days_remove = 90
		cost = 50

		available = {
			NOT = { check_variable = { gdp_per_capita < 25 } }
			has_idea = PER_brain_drain_5
 			hidden_trigger = { has_country_flag = PER_incapable_brain_drain }
		}
		complete_effect = {
		set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -2 }
		modify_treasury_effect = yes
		}
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision PER_brain_drain_removal_4"
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = PER_brain_drain_5
					add_idea = PER_brain_drain_4
				}
			}
		}
	PER_brain_drain_removal_3 = {

		days_remove = 90
		cost = 50

		visible = {
		has_idea = PER_brain_drain_4
		}
		available = {

				}

					has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_4

	PER_decrease_self_humiliation_level = {

		icon = GFX_decision_fist

		days_remove = 5
		days_re_enable = 3
		cost = 200

		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = PER_start_the_islamic_propaganda
			OR = {
				has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_1
				has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_2
				has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_3
				has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_4
				has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_5
				has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_6
				has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_7
				has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_8
				has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_9
				has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_10
			}

		}
		allowed = {
			original_tag = PER
		}
		available = {
			#check_variable = { treasury < 5 }
			AND = {
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = PER_seda_o_sima_decision
						has_country_flag = PER_road_billboard_decision
						has_country_flag = PER_social_media_decision
						has_country_flag = PER_tehran_military_parade_decision
						has_country_flag = PER_shiraz_military_parade_decision
						has_country_flag = PER_mashhad_military_parade_decision
						has_country_flag = PER_ahvaz_military_parade_decision
						has_country_flag = PER_tabriz_military_parade_decision
						has_country_flag = PER_isfahan_military_parade_decision
					}
				}
				AND = {
					check_variable = {
						var = islamic_propaganda_status
						value = 100
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -5 }
			modify_treasury_effect = yes
			set_country_flag = PER_decrease_self_humiliation_level_decision
		}

		remove_effect = {
			add_to_variable = {
				var = islamic_propaganda_status
				value = 10
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_10
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_10
					add_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_9
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_9
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_9
					add_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_8
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_8
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_8
					add_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_7
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_7
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_7
					add_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_6
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_6
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_6
					add_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_5
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_5
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_5
					add_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_4
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_4
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_4
					add_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_3
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_3
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_3
					add_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_2
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_2
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_2
					add_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_1
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_1
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_1
					add_idea = PER_unity_of_the_nation
				}
			}
			clear_variable = islamic_propaganda_status
			set_variable = { islamic_propaganda_status = 0 }
			clr_country_flag = PER_decrease_self_humiliation_level_decision
		}
	}
}

PER_resitance_axis = {
	PER_ask_hezbollah_to_start_a_border_war = {

		days_remove = 0
		days_re_enable = 100
		cost = 20

		visible = {
			HEZ = {
				is_ally_with = PER
			}
			country_exists = ISR
			ISR = {
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = HEZ
					has_border_war_with = HEZ
					is_ally_with = PER
					has_war_with = HEZ
				}
			}
		}

		allowed = {
			original_tag = PER
		}

		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision PER_ask_hezbollah_to_start_a_border_war"
			HEZ = {
				country_event = {
					id = axis_of_resistance_events.4
					days = 0
				}
			}
		}
	}
	PER_invite_syria = {

		days_remove = 0
		days_re_enable = 100
		cost = 25

		visible = {
			SYR = {
				is_in_faction = no
				has_government = communism
				has_idea = shia
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = PER
				}
			}
		}

		available = {
			SYR = {
				has_idea = shia
				OR = {
					emerging_autocracy_are_in_power = yes
					nationalist_military_junta_are_in_power = yes
				}
			}
			has_opinion = { target = SYR value > 9 }
			SYR = {

PER_majlis = {
	#
	PER_puppet_the_majlis = {
		allowed = { original_tag = PER }
		fire_only_once = yes
		available = {
			check_variable = {
				PER_majlis_support > 230
			}
			hidden_trigger = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = PER_MAJLIS_GIVEN_AWAY
				}
			}
		}
		visible = {
			check_variable = {
				PER_majlis_support > 230
			}
			has_country_flag = PER_influence_majlis
			NOT = { has_country_flag = PER_controlled_majlis }
		}
		cost = 500
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision PER_bureau_open"
			set_country_flag = PER_controlled_majlis
			clr_country_flag = PER_influence_majlis
			###
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						western_liberals_are_in_power = yes
						western_social_democrats_are_in_power = yes
						neutrality_neutral_libertarians_are_in_power = yes
					}
				}
				clr_country_flag = PER_conservative_majlis
				clr_country_flag = PER_nationalist_majlis
				clr_country_flag = PER_leftist_majlis
				clr_country_flag = PER_liberal_majlis
				set_country_flag = PER_liberal_majlis
			}
			#
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						emerging_communist_state_are_in_power = yes
						emerging_anarchist_communism_are_in_power = yes
						neutrality_neutral_social_are_in_power = yes
						neutrality_neutral_communism_are_in_power = yes
					}
				}
				clr_country_flag = PER_conservative_majlis
				clr_country_flag = PER_nationalist_majlis
				clr_country_flag = PER_liberal_majlis
				clr_country_flag = PER_leftist_majlis
				set_country_flag = PER_leftist_majlis
			}
			#
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						nationalist_monarchists_are_in_power = yes
						nationalist_military_junta_are_in_power = yes
						nationalist_fascist_are_in_power = yes
						nationalist_right_wing_populists_are_in_power = yes
					}
				}
				clr_country_flag = PER_conservative_majlis
				clr_country_flag = PER_leftist_majlis
				clr_country_flag = PER_liberal_majlis
				clr_country_flag = PER_nationalist_majlis
				set_country_flag = PER_nationalist_majlis
			}
			#
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						neutrality_neutral_conservatism_are_in_power = yes
						western_conservatism_are_in_power = yes
						western_autocrats_are_in_power = yes
					}
				}
				clr_country_flag = PER_nationalist_majlis
				clr_country_flag = PER_leftist_majlis
				clr_country_flag = PER_liberal_majlis
				clr_country_flag = PER_conservative_majlis
				set_country_flag = PER_conservative_majlis
			}
			# # # # #
			if = {
				limit = {
					emerging_hardline_shiite_are_in_power = yes
				}
				clr_country_flag = PER_nationalist_majlis
				clr_country_flag = PER_leftist_majlis
				clr_country_flag = PER_liberal_majlis
				clr_country_flag = PER_reformist_majlis
				clr_country_flag = PER_conservative_majlis
				set_country_flag = PER_principalist_majlis
			}
			#
			if = {
				limit = {
					emerging_moderate_shiite_are_in_power = yes
				}
				clr_country_flag = PER_nationalist_majlis
				clr_country_flag = PER_leftist_majlis
				clr_country_flag = PER_liberal_majlis
				clr_country_flag = PER_principalist_majlis
				clr_country_flag = PER_conservative_majlis
				set_country_flag = PER_reformist_majlis
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = PER_majlis_support
				value = 290
			}
			clr_country_flag = PER_majlis_block
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}

			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision PER_invite_clerics_to_the_government"
			add_power_balance_value = {
				id = PER_clergy_balance_of_power_category
				value = 0.10
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			political_power_gain = 0.15
			bureaucracy_cost_multiplier_modifier = 0.20
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 10
		}
	}
}

PER_revolutionary_council_formation = {
	PER_convince_pahlavi = {
		cost = 100
		visible = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = PER_PLAYING_PAHLAVI
					has_country_flag = PER_PAHLAVI_JOINED
				}
			}
		}
		available = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_decision = PER_convince_boroumand
					has_decision = PER_convince_pezeshkpour
				}
			}
		}
		fire_only_once = yes
		days_remove = 20
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision PER_convince_pahlavi"

			}
		}

		}

PER_Iranian_prime_ministers_elections = {
	# Conservatives
	PER_appoint_hashem_sabbaghian = {
		cost = 300
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = PER_minister_selection
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = PER_hashem_sabbaghian_minister
			}
		}
		fire_only_once = yes
		days_remove = 0
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision PER_appoint_hashem_sabbaghian"
			clr_country_flag = PER_minister_selection
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = PER_nationalist_majlis
						#has_country_flag = PER_conservative_majlis
						has_country_flag = PER_liberal_majlis
						has_country_flag = PER_leftist_majlis
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = PER_lose_some_election1
				add_to_variable = { PER_majlis_support = -15 }
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision PER_appoint_hashem_sabbaghian"
			hidden_effect = {
				add_ideas = PER_sabbaghian_idea
			}
			# Clear current Prime Minister
			PER_minister_clear = yes
			# Prime Minister Flag
			set_country_flag = PER_hashem_sabbaghian_minister
			# Update GUI
			add_to_variable = { iranian_president_change = 1 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = PER_sabbaghian_gets_appointed
			newline = yes
			custom_effect_tooltip = PER_sabbaghian_modifiers
			#
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = PER_appointed_pm
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = PER_appointed_pm
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 10
		}
	}

			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision PER_appoint_reza_pirzadeh"
			clr_country_flag = PER_minister_selection
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						#has_country_flag = PER_nationalist_majlis
						has_country_flag = PER_conservative_majlis
						has_country_flag = PER_liberal_majlis
						has_country_flag = PER_leftist_majlis
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = PER_lose_some_election1
				add_to_variable = { PER_majlis_support = -15 }
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision PER_appoint_reza_pirzadeh"
			hidden_effect = {
				add_ideas = PER_zahedi_idea
			}
			# Clear current Prime Minister
			PER_minister_clear = yes
			# Prime Minister Flag
			set_country_flag = PER_reza_pirzadeh_minister
			# Update GUI
			add_to_variable = { iranian_president_change = 1 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = PER_pirzadeh_gets_appointed
			newline = yes
			custom_effect_tooltip = PER_zahedi_modifiers
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = PER_appointed_pm
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = PER_appointed_pm
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 10
		}
	}
